<script>
    window.addEventListener('load', function () {
        const announcementBar = document.getElementById('announcement-bar');
        const messages = [
            document.getElementById('message1'),
            document.getElementById('message2'),
            document.getElementById('message3'),
 document.getElementById('message4'),
        ];

        // Retrieve the last shown message index from localStorage
        let currentIndex = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('currentMessageIndex') || '0', 10);

        // Hide all messages initially
        messages.forEach((message) => {
            message.style.display = 'none';
        });

        // Show the current message
        messages[currentIndex].style.display = 'flex';

        // Show the announcement bar
        setTimeout(() => {
            announcementBar.style.display = 'flex';
            document.body.classList.add('with-announcement');
        }, 10000); // 10-second delay

        // Update the index for the next page load
        currentIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % messages.length;
        localStorage.setItem('currentMessageIndex', currentIndex);

        // Close button functionality
        document.getElementById('close-announcement').addEventListener('click', function () {
            announcementBar.style.display = 'none';
            document.body.classList.remove('with-announcement');
        });
    });
</script>

						<div data-elementor-type="single-post" data-elementor-id="29249" class="elementor elementor-29249 elementor-location-single post-10765 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-malware category-osint category-phishing tag-cybercrime tag-malware tag-osint ast-article-single" data-elementor-post-type="elementor_library">
					<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-4434dc4 elementor-section-stretched news_ticker h-42 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="4434dc4" data-element_type="section" data-settings="{&quot;stretch_section&quot;:&quot;section-stretched&quot;,&quot;animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;,&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
							<div class="elementor-background-overlay"></div>
							<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-b70d168 ticker_col" data-id="b70d168" data-element_type="column" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0f4e9ff ticker_head elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="0f4e9ff" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"><span style="color:#fff;font-family: 'Poppins', sans-serif">TRENDING </span></h2>				</div>

			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-1fc9eff elementor-widget elementor-widget-html" data-id="1fc9eff" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="html.default">
					<div class="scroll"></div><div class="text-marquee"><div class="text-single"></div></div>
<style>

    * :focus { outline: 0; }
        .scroll {
    height: 1vh;
    font-size: 1rem;
    display: flex;
    justify-content: center;
    align-items: center;
  }
    
    .text-marquee {
    
      position: relative;
      display: flex;
      align-items: center;
      overflow-x: hidden;
    
    }
     
    .text-single {
      position: relative;
      white-space: pre;
      padding: 0;
      margin: 0;
      will-change: transform;
    background: #000;
    }
     
    .text {
    
      padding: 0;
      display: inline-block;
      margin-right: 2.8rem;
     font-family: 'Poppins',sans-serif; 
     font-weight: 400; 
     font-size: 14px;
     color: #fff;
    }
    .values:focus,.values:active{
        border:none;
        outline: 0;
    }
    .values .text{
        margin-left: 2px;
        margin-right: 3px;
    }
    .keys .text{
        margin-right: 5px;
        margin-left: 2.8rem;
        font-weight: bold;
    }
  
    .text-single a:last-child .text{
         padding-right: 2.8rem!important; 
    }
    
    
      .text.js-text:hover, .text.js-text:active, .text.js-text:focus{
         outline: 0 none;
      -moz-outline: 0 none;
      }  
      
    </style>
<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.6.0/jquery.min.js?ver<%=DateTime.Now.Ticks.ToString()%>" type="text/javascript"></script>
  
  
  
  <script src="https://unpkg.co/gsap@3/dist/gsap.min.js?ver<%=DateTime.Now.Ticks.ToString()%>" type="text/javascript"></script>
  
  
  
  <script src="https://unpkg.com/gsap@3/dist/Draggable.min.js?ver<%=DateTime.Now.Ticks.ToString()%>" type="text/javascript"></script>
  
  
  <script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
      let loops = gsap.utils.toArray('.text-single').map((line, i) => {
          const links = line.querySelectorAll(".js-text"),
              tl = horizontalLoop(links, {
                  repeat: -1,
                  speed: 1 + i * 0.5,
                  draggable: true,
                  reversed: false,
                  paddingRight: parseFloat(gsap.getProperty(links[0], "marginRight", "px"))
              });
          links.forEach(link => {
              link.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => gsap.to(tl, {timeScale: 0, overwrite: true}));
              link.addEventListener("mouseleave", () => gsap.to(tl, {timeScale: i ? -1 : 1, overwrite: true}));
          });
      });
  
      let currentScroll = 0;
      let scrollDirection = 1;
  
      window.addEventListener("scroll", () => {
          let direction = (window.pageYOffset > currentScroll) ? 1 : -1;
          if (direction !== scrollDirection) {
              loops.forEach(tl => gsap.to(tl, {timeScale: direction, overwrite: true}));
              scrollDirection = direction;
          }
          currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;
      });
  
    function horizontalLoop(items, config) {
      items = gsap.utils.toArray(items);
      config = config || {};
      let tl = gsap.timeline({repeat: config.repeat, paused: config.paused, defaults: {ease: "none"}, onReverseComplete: () => tl.totalTime(tl.rawTime() + tl.duration() * 100)}),
          length = items.length,
          startX = items[0].offsetLeft,
          times = [],
          widths = [],
          xPercents = [],
          curIndex = 0,
          pixelsPerSecond = (config.speed || 1) * 100,
          snap = config.snap === false ? v => v : gsap.utils.snap(config.snap || 1), // some browsers shift by a pixel to accommodate flex layouts, so for example if width is 20% the first element's width might be 242px, and the next 243px, alternating back and forth. So we snap to 5 percentage points to make things look more natural
          populateWidths = () => items.forEach((el, i) => {
        widths[i] = parseFloat(gsap.getProperty(el, "width", "px"));
        xPercents[i] = snap(parseFloat(gsap.getProperty(el, "x", "px")) / widths[i] * 100 + gsap.getProperty(el, "xPercent"));
      }),
      getTotalWidth = () => items[length-1].offsetLeft + xPercents[length-1] / 100 * widths[length-1] - startX + items[length-1].offsetWidth * gsap.getProperty(items[length-1], "scaleX") + (parseFloat(config.paddingRight) || 0),
        totalWidth, curX, distanceToStart, distanceToLoop, item, i;
      populateWidths();
    gsap.set(items, { // convert "x" to "xPercent" to make things responsive, and populate the widths/xPercents Arrays to make lookups faster.
          xPercent: i => xPercents[i]
      });
      gsap.set(items, {x: 0});
      totalWidth = getTotalWidth();
      for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
          item = items[i];
          curX = xPercents[i] / 100 * widths[i];
          distanceToStart = item.offsetLeft + curX - startX;
          distanceToLoop = distanceToStart + widths[i] * gsap.getProperty(item, "scaleX");
          tl.to(item, {xPercent: snap((curX - distanceToLoop) / widths[i] * 100), duration: distanceToLoop / pixelsPerSecond}, 0)
            .fromTo(item, {xPercent: snap((curX - distanceToLoop + totalWidth) / widths[i] * 100)}, {xPercent: xPercents[i], duration: (curX - distanceToLoop + totalWidth - curX) / pixelsPerSecond, immediateRender: false}, distanceToLoop / pixelsPerSecond)
            .add("label" + i, distanceToStart / pixelsPerSecond);
          times[i] = distanceToStart / pixelsPerSecond;
      }
      function toIndex(index, vars) {
          vars = vars || {};
          (Math.abs(index - curIndex) > length / 2) && (index += index > curIndex ? -length : length); // always go in the shortest direction
          let newIndex = gsap.utils.wrap(0, length, index),
              time = times[newIndex];
          if (time > tl.time() !== index > curIndex) { // if we're wrapping the timeline's playhead, make the proper adjustments
              vars.modifiers = {time: gsap.utils.wrap(0, tl.duration())};
              time += tl.duration() * (index > curIndex ? 1 : -1);
          }
          curIndex = newIndex;
          vars.overwrite = true;
          return tl.tweenTo(time, vars);
      }
      tl.next = vars => toIndex(curIndex+1, vars);
      tl.previous = vars => toIndex(curIndex-1, vars);
      tl.current = () => curIndex;
      tl.toIndex = (index, vars) => toIndex(index, vars);
    tl.updateIndex = () => curIndex = Math.round(tl.progress() * (items.length - 1));
      tl.times = times;
    tl.progress(1, true).progress(0, true); // pre-render for performance
    if (config.reversed) {
      tl.vars.onReverseComplete();
      tl.reverse();
    }
    if (config.draggable && typeof(Draggable) === "function") {
      let proxy = document.createElement("div"),
          wrap = gsap.utils.wrap(0, 1),
          ratio, startProgress, draggable, dragSnap, roundFactor,
          align = () => tl.progress(wrap(startProgress + (draggable.startX - draggable.x) * ratio)),
          syncIndex = () => tl.updateIndex();
      typeof(InertiaPlugin) === "undefined" && console.warn("InertiaPlugin required for momentum-based scrolling and snapping. https://greensock.com/club");
      draggable = Draggable.create(proxy, {
        trigger: items[0].parentNode,
        type: "x",
        onPress() {
          startProgress = tl.progress();
          tl.progress(0);
          populateWidths();
          totalWidth = getTotalWidth();
          ratio = 1 / totalWidth;
          dragSnap = totalWidth / items.length;
          roundFactor = Math.pow(10, ((dragSnap + "").split(".")[1] || "").length);
          tl.progress(startProgress);
        },
        onDrag: align,
        onThrowUpdate: align,
        inertia: true,
        snap: value => {
          let n = Math.round(parseFloat(value) / dragSnap) * dragSnap * roundFactor;
          return (n - n % 1) / roundFactor;
        },
        onRelease: syncIndex,
        onThrowComplete: () => gsap.set(proxy, {x: 0}) && syncIndex()
      })[0];
    }
    
      return tl;
  }
  });
  </script>

				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3c220676 elementor-widget elementor-widget-theme-post-title elementor-page-title elementor-widget-heading" data-id="3c220676" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="theme-post-title.default">
					<h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Emotet Returns With New TTPs And delivers .lnk files to its victims</h1>				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-1fcc1d6c elementor-widget elementor-widget-theme-post-excerpt" data-id="1fcc1d6c" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="theme-post-excerpt.default">
					The .lnk file further executes VBScript or PowerShell script to download the Emotet payload in the victims' machine. 				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2907e1e2 blog_content elementor-widget elementor-widget-theme-post-content" data-id="2907e1e2" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="theme-post-content.default">
							<div data-elementor-type="wp-post" data-elementor-id="10765" class="elementor elementor-10765" data-elementor-post-type="post">
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-cbc6cc7 e-flex e-con-boxed e-con e-parent" data-id="cbc6cc7" data-element_type="container">
					<div class="e-con-inner">
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7f72ddc2 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="7f72ddc2" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
									
<p>On 2024-04-22, the <a href="https://twitter.com/malware_traffic/status/1517622327000846338" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">@malware_traffic</a> posted on their Twitter handle that the epoch4 Emotet server started spamming and delivering zipped .lnk files to its victims through spam email, as shown in Figure 1. The .lnk file further executes VBScript or PowerShell script to download the Emotet payload in the victims&#8217; machine. The use of a .lnk file and PowerShell or VBScript is a new combination that has not been used by the Emotet before.</p>

<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="490" height="421" data-attachment-id="10768" data-permalink="https://cyble.com/blog/emotet-returns-with-new-ttps-and-delivers-lnk-files-to-its-victims/figure-1-spam-email/" data-orig-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-1-Spam-Email.png" data-orig-size="490,421" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Figure-1-Spam-Email" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-1-Spam-Email-300x258.png" data-large-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-1-Spam-Email.png" class="wp-image-10768" src="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-1-Spam-Email.png" alt="Emotet" title="Emotet Returns With New TTPs And delivers .lnk files to its victims 7" srcset="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-1-Spam-Email.png 490w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-1-Spam-Email-300x258.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 490px) 100vw, 490px" />
<figcaption>Figure 1 &#8211; Spam Email</figcaption>
</figure>

<p>The Cyble Research Labs has already published a <a href="https://cyble.com/2022/02/26/emotet-malware-back-in-action/" target="_blank">blog</a> about Emotet TTPs in  February 2022. During this time, the Emotet was delivered to users with a spam email containing an MS excel attachment.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Technical Analysis</strong></h2>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-infection-chain-1"><strong>Infection Chain-1</strong></h3>

<p>SHA256: <strong>115d7891a2abbe038c12ccc9ed3cfeedfdd1242e51bcc67bfa22c7cc2567fb10</strong></p><!-- This site is converting visitors into subscribers and customers with OptinMonster - https://optinmonster.com :: Campaign Title: Request demo blog -->

<!-- / OptinMonster -->

<p>The initial infection starts when the user extracts the password-protected zip file and executes the link file in the machine. Upon execution, the .lnk file has commands to drop a malicious VB script file in the Temp location of the target machine, as shown in the below figure.</p>

<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="385" height="519" data-attachment-id="10769" data-permalink="https://cyble.com/blog/emotet-returns-with-new-ttps-and-delivers-lnk-files-to-its-victims/figure-2-command-to-drop-vbscript/" data-orig-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript.png" data-orig-size="385,519" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript-223x300.png" data-large-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript.png" class="wp-image-10769" src="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript.png" alt="Emotet" title="Emotet Returns With New TTPs And delivers .lnk files to its victims 8" srcset="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript.png 385w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-2-Command-to-Drop-VBScript-223x300.png 223w" sizes="(max-width: 385px) 100vw, 385px" />
<figcaption>Figure 2 &#8211; Command to Drop VBScript</figcaption>
</figure>

<p>The dropped VB script further executes with the help of WScript.exe, downloads the Emotet payload from the remote server, and executes it using regsvr32.exe. The payload URLs are encoded using base64 and decoded during runtime for downloading the Emotet payload. The below Figure shows the VBS file.</p>

<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="602" height="244" data-attachment-id="10770" data-permalink="https://cyble.com/blog/emotet-returns-with-new-ttps-and-delivers-lnk-files-to-its-victims/figure-3-downloads-and-executes-payload/" data-orig-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload.png" data-orig-size="602,244" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload-300x122.png" data-large-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload.png" class="wp-image-10770" src="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload.png" alt="Emotet" title="Emotet Returns With New TTPs And delivers .lnk files to its victims 9" srcset="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload.png 602w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload-600x243.png 600w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-3-Downloads-and-Executes-Payload-300x122.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 602px) 100vw, 602px" />
<figcaption>Figure 3 &#8211; Downloads and Executes Payload</figcaption>
</figure>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-infection-chain-2"><strong>Infection Chain-2</strong></h3>

<h4 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-sha256-09f44c33ba0a5f1e22cd5b8b0d40c9808e2668ee9050ac855a6ae0744bc9e924">SHA256:<strong>09f44c33ba0a5f1e22cd5b8b0d40c9808e2668ee9050ac855a6ae0744bc9e924</strong></h4>

<p>On 2024-04-26, the Emotet campaigns started using .lnk and PowerShell combinations for delivering the payloads. In this campaign, the .lnk file drops a PowerShell file in the Temp folder, which further downloads the Emotet payload from the remote server and executes it using regsvr32.exe. The below Figure shows the PowerShell command used by the malware.</p>

<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="602" height="198" data-attachment-id="10772" data-permalink="https://cyble.com/blog/emotet-returns-with-new-ttps-and-delivers-lnk-files-to-its-victims/figure-5-downloads-and-execute-emotet-payload/" data-orig-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload.png" data-orig-size="602,198" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload-300x99.png" data-large-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload.png" class="wp-image-10772" src="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload.png" alt="Emotet" title="Emotet Returns With New TTPs And delivers .lnk files to its victims 11" srcset="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload.png 602w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload-600x197.png 600w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-5-–-Downloads-and-Execute-Emotet-Payload-300x99.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 602px) 100vw, 602px" />
<figcaption>Figure 5 – Downloads and Execute Emotet Payload</figcaption>
</figure>

<p>The below Figure depicts the execution flow of Emotet malware through PowerShell.</p>

<figure class="wp-block-image aligncenter size-full"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="591" height="83" data-attachment-id="10773" data-permalink="https://cyble.com/blog/emotet-returns-with-new-ttps-and-delivers-lnk-files-to-its-victims/figure-6-execution-flowthrough-powershell/" data-orig-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell.png" data-orig-size="591,83" data-comments-opened="0" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell-300x42.png" data-large-file="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell.png" class="wp-image-10773" src="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell.png" alt="Emotet" title="Emotet Returns With New TTPs And delivers .lnk files to its victims 12" srcset="https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell.png 591w, https://cyble.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/04/Figure-6-Execution-FlowThrough-PowerShell-300x42.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 591px) 100vw, 591px" />
<figcaption>Figure 6 &#8211; Execution FlowThrough PowerShell</figcaption>
</figure>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="h-conclusion"><strong>Conclusion</strong></h2>

<p>Emotet is a sophisticated and long-lasting <a href="https://cyble.com/knowledge-hub/what-is-malware/" target="_blank">malware</a> that has impacted users globally. <a href="https://cyble.com/knowledge-hub/cyber-threat-actor-and-types/" target="_blank">Threat Actors</a> are constantly adapting their techniques to stay one step of cybersecurity entities – Emotet is one such example. Cyble Research Labs is continuously monitoring the activity of Emotet and other malware and will keep our readers updated.</p>

<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Our Recommendations</strong></h2>

<p>We have listed some essential <a href="https://cyble.com/knowledge-hub/cybersecurity/" target="_blank">cybersecurity</a> best practices that create the first line of control against attackers. We recommend that our readers follow the best practices given below:  </p>

<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Don’t keep important files in common locations such as the Desktop, My Documents, etc.</li>
<li>Use strong passwords and enforce multi-factor authentication wherever possible.</li>
<li>​Turn on the automatic software update feature on your computer, mobile, and other connected devices wherever possible and pragmatic.</li>
<li>​Use a reputed anti-virus and Internet security software package on your connected devices, including PC, laptop, and mobile.   </li>
<li>​Refrain from opening untrusted links and email attachments without verifying their authenticity.</li>
<li>​Conduct regular backup practices and keep those backups offline or in a separate network. </li>
</ul>

<script>
   let autoHideTimeout;

document.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    var scrollPosition = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
    var documentHeight = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;

    // Calculate scroll percentage
    var scrollPercentage = (scrollPosition / documentHeight) * 100;

    // Check if the screen width is greater than 768px (for non-mobile devices)
    if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
        // Only activate the slider when scroll is between 60% and 100%
        if (scrollPercentage >= 60 && scrollPercentage <= 100) {
            // Show the slider by sliding it in
            document.getElementById('rightSlider').classList.add('active');

            // Clear any previous auto-hide timer
            clearTimeout(autoHideTimeout);

            // Set a 5-second timer to auto-slide the slider back out
            autoHideTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
                document.getElementById('rightSlider').classList.remove('active');
            }, 5000); // 5000 milliseconds = 5 seconds
        } else {
            // If not within 60% - 100% range, hide the slider
            document.getElementById('rightSlider').classList.remove('active');
        }
    }
});

document.getElementById('rightSlider').addEventListener('mouseover', function() {
    // On mouseover, keep the slider active and clear the auto-hide timer
    clearTimeout(autoHideTimeout);
    this.classList.add('active');
});

document.getElementById('rightSlider').addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
    // On mouse leave, start the auto-hide timer again for 5 seconds
    clearTimeout(autoHideTimeout);
    autoHideTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
        document.getElementById('rightSlider').classList.remove('active');
    }, 5000); // 5000 milliseconds = 5 seconds
});

</script>				</div>

				(function() {
					// Global page view and session tracking for UAEL Modal Popup feature
					try {
						// Session tracking: increment if this is a new session
						
						// Check if any popup on this page uses current page tracking
						var hasCurrentPageTracking = false;
						var currentPagePopups = [];
						// Check all modal popups on this page for current page tracking
						if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
							jQuery('.uael-modal-parent-wrapper').each(function() {
								var scope = jQuery(this).data('page-views-scope');
								var enabled = jQuery(this).data('page-views-enabled');
								var popupId = jQuery(this).attr('id').replace('-overlay', '');	
								if (enabled === 'yes' && scope === 'current') {
									hasCurrentPageTracking = true;
									currentPagePopups.push(popupId);
								}
							});
						}
						// Global tracking: ALWAYS increment if ANY popup on the site uses global tracking
												// Current page tracking: increment per-page counters
						if (hasCurrentPageTracking && currentPagePopups.length > 0) {
							var currentUrl = window.location.href;
							var urlKey = 'uael_page_views_' + btoa(currentUrl).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '').substring(0, 50);
							var currentPageViews = parseInt(localStorage.getItem(urlKey) || '0');
							currentPageViews++;
							localStorage.setItem(urlKey, currentPageViews.toString());
							// Store URL mapping for each popup
							for (var i = 0; i < currentPagePopups.length; i++) {
								var popupUrlKey = 'uael_popup_' + currentPagePopups[i] + '_url_key';
								localStorage.setItem(popupUrlKey, urlKey);
							}
						}
					} catch (e) {
						// Silently fail if localStorage is not available
					}
				})();
				</script>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );

								jQuery.cachedScript = function( url, options ) {
									// Allow user to set any option except for dataType, cache, and url.
									options = jQuery.extend( options || {}, {
										dataType: "script",
										cache: true,
										url: url
									});
									// Return the jqXHR object so we can chain callbacks.
									return jQuery.ajax( options );
								};
							    jQuery( window ).on( "elementor/frontend/init", function() {
									elementorFrontend.hooks.addAction( "frontend/element_ready/global", function( $scope, $ ){
										if ( "undefined" == typeof $scope ) {
												return;
										}
										if ( $scope.hasClass( "uael-particle-yes" ) ) {
											window.scope_array.push( $scope );
											$scope.find(".uael-particle-wrapper").addClass("js-is-enabled");

											return;
										}
										if(elementorFrontend.isEditMode() && $scope.find(".uael-particle-wrapper").hasClass("js-is-enabled") && window.backend == 0 ){
											var uael_url = uael_particles_script.uael_particles_url;

											jQuery.cachedScript( uael_url );
											window.backend = 1;
										}else if(elementorFrontend.isEditMode()){
											var uael_url = uael_particles_script.uael_particles_url;
											jQuery.cachedScript( uael_url ).done(function(){
												var flag = true;
											});
										}
									});
								});

								// Define cachedScript globally to avoid redefining it.

								jQuery.cachedScript = function(url, options) {
									options = jQuery.extend(options || {}, {
										dataType: "script",
										cache: true,
										url: url
									});

										loadParticleScript();
								});

								jQuery( window ).one( "elementor/frontend/init", () => {
								 	if (!uael_particle_loaded) {
